internal), `SignatureType` (grafana, commercial, community, private, private-glob), `Signature` struct, and signature-related error codes/types.\\n\\n**Interfaces** (`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`): Defines the core interfaces: `SignatureCalculator` (calculates signature state for a plugin), `KeyRetriever` (fetches PGP public keys), `KeyStore` (caches public keys), and `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` (decides whether unsigned plugins may load).\\n\\n**Manifest Signing & Verification** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`): The central implementation. `PluginManifest` holds the signed manifest structure (plugin ID, version, keyId, file hashes, signature type, root URLs). The `Signature` struct implements `SignatureCalculator`. `ReadPluginManifestFromFS` reads MANIFEST.txt from the plugin filesystem. `readPluginManifest` PGP-decodes the clearsign block and calls `validateManifest`. `validateManifest` checks required fields and calls `Verify` to check the PGP signature against the retrieved public key. `Calculate` orchestrates: reads manifest, checks V2, validates ID/version match, checks root URLs via `urlMatch`, verifies file hashes via `verifyHash`, and checks for unsigned files.\\n\\n**Signature Validation on Load** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`): `Validation` implements `ValidateSignature`, which checks whether the plugin's computed signature state is valid. For child plugins it inherits parent signature. For unsigned plugins it delegates to `PluginLoaderAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin`.\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`): `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin` permits an unsigned plugin if: dev mode is enabled, or the plugin ID is in `cfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned` (the `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` config list).\\n\\n**Static PGP Public Key** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Hard-coded Grafana public key (ID `7e4d0c6a708866e7`) used when dynamic key download is disabled.\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retrieval** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the grafana.com API (`/plugins/ci/keys`), refreshing every 10 days. Falls back to the static key if the store is empty.\\n\\n**Key Retriever Service** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`): Wires dynamic vs. static key retriever based on `PluginSkipPublicKeyDownload` setting.\\n\\n**Validation Pipeline Step** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): `PluginSignatureValidator` wraps `signature.Validator` as a pipeline `ValidateFunc`. `DefaultValidateFuncs` assembles it with the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`. `SignatureValidationStep` creates the validate func.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/validation.go`): `Validate` stage runs all `ValidateFunc`s including signature validation.\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): `DefaultConstructor.Construct` calls `SignatureCalculator.Calculate` during plugin construction to attach the signature state before validation.\\n\\n**Integration Layer** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`, `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/pipeline.go`): `SignatureValidation` / `SignatureValidationStep` (integration version) records errors on the plugin. `ProvideValidationStage` and `ProvideBootstrapStage` wire everything together via dependency injection.\\n\\n**Configuration** internal), `SignatureType` (grafana, commercial, community, private, private-glob), `Signature` struct, and signature-related error codes/types.\\n\\n**Interfaces** (`pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`): Defines the core interfaces: `SignatureCalculator` (calculates signature state for a plugin), `KeyRetriever` (fetches PGP public keys), `KeyStore` (caches public keys), and `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` (decides whether unsigned plugins may load).\\n\\n**Manifest Signing & Verification** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`): The central implementation. `PluginManifest` holds the signed manifest structure (plugin ID, version, keyId, file hashes, signature type, root URLs). The `Signature` struct implements `SignatureCalculator`. `ReadPluginManifestFromFS` reads MANIFEST.txt from the plugin filesystem. `readPluginManifest` PGP-decodes the clearsign block and calls `validateManifest`. `validateManifest` checks required fields and calls `Verify` to check the PGP signature against the retrieved public key. `Calculate` orchestrates: reads manifest, checks V2, validates ID/version match, checks root URLs via `urlMatch`, verifies file hashes via `verifyHash`, and checks for unsigned files.\\n\\n**Signature Validation on Load** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`): `Validation` implements `ValidateSignature`, which checks whether the plugin's computed signature state is valid. For child plugins it inherits parent signature. For unsigned plugins it delegates to `PluginLoaderAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin`.\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`): `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer.CanLoadPlugin` permits an unsigned plugin if: dev mode is enabled, or the plugin ID is in `cfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned` (the `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` config list).\\n\\n**Static PGP Public Key** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Hard-coded Grafana public key (ID `7e4d0c6a708866e7`) used when dynamic key download is disabled.\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retrieval** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the grafana.com API (`/plugins/ci/keys`), refreshing every 10 days. Falls back to the static key if the store is empty.\\n\\n**Key Retriever Service** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go`): Wires dynamic vs. static key retriever based on `PluginSkipPublicKeyDownload` setting.\\n\\n**Validation Pipeline Step** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): `PluginSignatureValidator` wraps `signature.Validator` as a pipeline `ValidateFunc`. `DefaultValidateFuncs` assembles it with the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer`. `SignatureValidationStep` creates the validate func.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/validation.go`): `Validate` stage runs all `ValidateFunc`s including signature validation.\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): `DefaultConstructor.Construct` calls `SignatureCalculator.Calculate` during plugin construction to attach the signature state before validation.\\n\\n**Integration Layer** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`, `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/pipeline.go`): `SignatureValidation` / `SignatureValidationStep` (integration version) records errors on the plugin. `ProvideValidationStage` and `ProvideBootstrapStage` wire everything together via dependency injection.\\n\\n**Configuration** (`pkg/plugins/config/config.go`, `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginconfig/config.go`, `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go`): `PluginManagementCfg.PluginsAllowUnsigned` holds the allowlist. `readPluginSettings` reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` from grafana.ini. `ProvidePluginManagementConfig` bridges the setting into the plugin management config.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
